PRADEShIYA  SABhA  mAwAThAGAmA 
It is hereby notified for public information that it has been adopted under resolution No. 5ii  moved at the General Conference 
held on 30.08.2022 at Pradeshiya Sabha Mawathagama  that all the roads and thoroughfares for which legal action had not 
been filed in a proper  judicial Court before the date specified  or roads and thoroughfares confirmed as the roads and thor-
oughfares that should be owned by Pradeshiya Sabha Mawathagama as per the Decree of a Judicial Court in which a case 
had been filed before the said date and not mentioned in the following schedule from among the roads and thoroughfares 
given in the list of the schedule of the notification published in the Gazette Paper No. 2271/30  and dated 15.03.2022  shall 
be confirmed as roads and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Mawathagama  in terms of orders made by the 
series of “ Orders on publication of notifications specifying preparation of plans and lists for roads and thoroughfares main-
tained by the Pradeshiya Sabha within the North Western Province” published by Extraordinary  Gazette Paper No. 2238/35 
and dated 30
th July 2021 by the Hon. Governor in the North Western Province and in terms of the order by Section 24(1) of 
Pradeshiya Sabha Act No. 15 0f 1987.
 S.K. AnurA KAmAl PererA,  
 Chairman,  
 Pradeshiya Sabha Mawathagama.
              
At Pradeshiya Sabha Mawathagama,
31st august, 2022.

Part IV (B) - GAZETTE EXTRAORDINARY OF THE DEMOCRATIC SOCIALIST REPUBLIC OF SRI LANKA - 09.09.2022
2aResolution
Pradeshiya Sabha Mawathagama  Proposes that the roads and thoroughfares for which legal actions had not been filed in a proper Judicial  Court and not mentioned 
in the following schedule from among the roads and thoroughfares given in the list of the schedule of the notification published in the Gazette Paper No. dated 
15.03.2022 according to the resolution No. 5.xiv made at the Pradeshiya Sabha conference held on 10.02.2022, shall be confirmed as roads and thoroughfares 
owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Mawathagama  in terms of orders made by the series of “ Orders on publication of notifications specifying preparation of plans and 
lists for roads and thoroughfares maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabha within the North Western Province” published by Extraordinary  Gazette Paper No. 2238/35 
and dated 30
th  July 2021 by the Hon. Governor in the North Western Province and in terms of the order by Section 24(1) of Pradeshiya Sabha Act No. 15 of 1987,
